\subsection{Detailed Description}
This file contains definitions of all images, cursors, colours, fonts and grids used by Audacity.

This will be split up into separate include files to reduce the amount of recompilation on a change.

Meantime, do N\+OT D\+E\+L\+E\+TE any of these declarations, even if they\textquotesingle{}re unused, as they\textquotesingle{}re all offset by prior declarations.

To add an image, you give its size and name like so\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}
\hyperlink{_macro_magic_8h_a2133710339e3f579a7d20fa573880bd0}{DEFINE\_IMAGE}( bmpPause, wxImage( 16, 16 ), wxT(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Pause"}));
\end{DoxyCode}


If you do this and run the program the image will be black to start with, but you can go into \hyperlink{class_theme_prefs}{Theme\+Prefs} and load it (load components) from there. Audacity will look for a file called \char`\"{}\+Pause.\+png\char`\"{}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Now save into Image\+Cache.
\item From here on you can get the image by loading Image\+Cache.
\item To burn it into the program defaults, use the \textquotesingle{}Output Sourcery\textquotesingle{} button.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Themability \hyperlink{latency_8c_a7d946209d777cb95fe30364b8d321207}{in} D\+Oxygen documentation \hyperlink{hashrout_8h_a63bdfbdfaa50cfc85afcbff4ce2c16a6}{for} more details.
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
